<p><a target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener" class="external text" href="http://onegame.gg/">One Game Agency</a> returns with season 3 of <b>AMD SAPPHIRE OGA Dota PIT China</b>, where eight of China’s best Dota 2 pro teams will go face to face for the title of the new champions as they compete for the $90,000 <abbr title="United States Dollar">USD</abbr> prize pool.<sup id="cite_ref-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-1">&#91;1&#93;</a></sup>
</p>

<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Format">Format</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/dota2/index.php?title=Dota_Pit_League/Online/3/China&amp;action=edit&amp;section=1" title="Edit section: Format">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<ul><li><b>Participants</b>
<ul><li>Eight invited teams</li></ul></li>
<li><b>Group Stage</b> - <i>September 29th - October 5th, 2020</i>
<ul><li>Two groups of four team</li>
<li>Single round-robin, all matches are <abbr title="Best-of-three">Bo3</abbr></li>
<li><span style="background-color:rgb(221,244,221);">Top team in each group</span> advance to the Upper Bracket R1 of the upper bracket</li>
<li><span style="background-color:rgb(229,244,198);">2nd and 3rd placed teams</span> advance to the Upper Bracket R2 of the upper bracket</li>
<li><span style="background-color:rgb(251,223,223);">Bottom team</span> in each group is eliminated</li>
<li><span class="mw-customtoggle-Tiebreaker" style="border-bottom:1px dotted;"><i>Click here for tiebreaker rules</i></span></li></ul></li></ul>
<div class="toccolours mw-collapsible mw-collapsed" id="mw-customcollapsible-Tiebreaker" style="width:760px; margin-left:45px">
<ol><li>Match results between tied teams</li>
<li>Map results between tied teams</li>
<li>Map results between all teams</li>
<li><abbr title="Best-of-one">Bo1</abbr> tiebreaker games</li>
<li>Shortest duration of tiebreaker games</li>
<li>Coin toss</li></ol>
</div>
<ul><li><b>Playoffs</b> - <i>October 6th - October 11th, 2020</i>
<ul><li>Double-elimination bracket</li>
<li>All matches except Grand Final are <abbr title="Best-of-three">Bo3</abbr></li>
<li>Grand Final is <abbr title="Best-of-five">Bo5</abbr>,</li></ul></li></ul>
